Emerging growth company&#160;<span style="font-family:Times New Roman"><ix:nonNumeric name="dei:EntityEmergingGrowthCompany" contextRef="duration_2022-12-13_to_2022-12-13" format="ixt-sec:boolballotbox">&#9744;</ix:nonNumeric></span></p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">If an emerging growth company, indicate by check mark if the registrant has Re-elected not to use the extended transition period for complying with any new or revised financial accounting standards provided pursuant to Section 13(a) of the Exchange Act. <span style="font-family:Times New Roman">&#9744;</span></p> <p style="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p> <p style="line-height:3.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:1px solid #000000">&#160;</p></div></div> <p style="page-break-before:always"></p> <hr style="color:#999999;height:3px;width:100%" /> <div style="text-align:center"> <div style="width:8.5in;text-align:left;margin-left: auto;margin-right: auto"> <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL;font-weight:bold">Item&#160;5.07. Submission of Matters to a Vote of Security Holders</p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">On December&#160;13, 2022, Microsoft Corporation (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) held its 2022 Annual Shareholders Meeting (the &#8220;Annual Meeting&#8221;). There were 7,456,502,484 shares of common stock entitled to be voted at the Annual Meeting, of which 6,407,164,715 were voted in person or by proxy. The results for each item submitted for a vote of shareholders are as follows. The shareholders:</p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">(1) Voted to elect each of the twelve (12)&#160;nominees for director.</p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">(2) Approved, on an advisory basis, the compensation of the Company&#8217;s named executive officers.</p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">(3) Voted to ratify the appointment of Deloitte&#160;&amp; Touche LLP as the Company&#8217;s independent registered public accounting firm for fiscal year 2023.</p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">(4) Did not approve a shareholder proposal concerning a cost/benefit analysis of diversity and inclusion.</p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">(5) Did not approve a shareholder proposal concerning a report on hiring of persons with arrest or incarceration records.</p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">(6) Did not approve a shareholder proposal concerning a report on investment of retirement funds in companies contributing to climate change</p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">(7) Did not approve a shareholder proposal concerning a report on<span style="font-weight:bold">&#160;</span>government use of Microsoft technology.</p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">(8) Did not approve a shareholder proposal concerning a report on development of products for the military.</p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">(9) Did not approve a shareholder proposal concerning a report on tax transparency.</p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">The Company&#8217;s inspector of election certified the following vote tabulations:</p> <p style="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL;font-weight:bold">Election of Directors</p> <p style="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>

if(e)e.style.display='block';Show.LastAR=e};Show.hideAR=function(){Show.LastAR.style.display='none'};Show.toggleNext=function(a){var e=a;while(e.nodeName!='DIV')e=e.nextSibling;if(!e.style){}else if(!e.style.display){}else{var d,p_;if(e.style.display=='none'){d='block';p='-'}else{d='none';p='+'}
